Website : http://www.tools4sql.net
Email : info@tools4sql.net
*/

SELECT  
		[dbo].[Orders].[OrderID],
		[dbo].[Orders].[CustomerID],
		[dbo].[Customers].[CompanyName] AS [Customers_CompanyName],
		[dbo].[Customers].[ContactName],
		[dbo].[Orders].[EmployeeID],
		[dbo].[Employees].[LastName],
		[dbo].[Employees].[FirstName],
		[dbo].[Orders].[OrderDate],
		[dbo].[Orders].[RequiredDate],
		[dbo].[Orders].[ShippedDate],
		[dbo].[Orders].[ShipVia],
		[dbo].[Shippers].[CompanyName] AS [Shippers_CompanyName],
		[dbo].[Orders].[Freight],
		[dbo].[Orders].[ShipName],
		[dbo].[Orders].[ShipAddress],
		[dbo].[Orders].[ShipCity],
		[dbo].[Orders].[ShipRegion],
		[dbo].[Orders].[ShipPostalCode],
		[dbo].[Orders].[ShipCountry]
FROM  [dbo].[Orders]
LEFT OUTER JOIN [dbo].[Customers]
ON [dbo].[Orders].[CustomerID] = [dbo].[Customers].[CustomerID]
LEFT OUTER JOIN [dbo].[Employees]
ON [dbo].[Orders].[EmployeeID] = [dbo].[Employees].[EmployeeID]
LEFT OUTER JOIN [dbo].[Shippers]
ON [dbo].[Orders].[ShipVia] = [dbo].[Shippers].[ShipperID]

ORDER BY [dbo].[Orders].[OrderDate]

GO

CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[PR_Region_Insert]

		@RegionID          		int OUTPUT,
		@RegionDescription 		nchar (50)

/*
This is SP Parameter Comment generated from Tools4SQL.net - T4S Stored Procedure Generator.
Website : http://www.tools4sql.net
Email : info@tools4sql.net
*/

AS

SET NOCOUNT ON;

/*
This is SP Body Comment generated from Tools4SQL.net - T4S Stored Procedure Generator.
Website : http://www.tools4sql.net
Email : info@tools4sql.net
*/

BEGIN TRY
BEGIN TRAN

SELECT @RegionID = ISNULL(MAX([RegionID]),0) + 1 FROM [dbo].[Region]


INSERT [dbo].[Region]
(
		[RegionID],
		[RegionDescription]
)
VALUES
(
		@RegionID,
		@RegionDescription
)

COMMIT TRAN
END TRY

BEGIN CATCH
ROLLBACK TRAN

DECLARE @ErrorSeverity_INT INT;

		[dbo].[titleview].[price],
		[dbo].[titleview].[ytd_sales],
		[dbo].[titleview].[pub_id]
FROM  [dbo].[titleview]

ORDER BY [dbo].[titleview].[title]

GO
--~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~
